\DoxyCodeLine{07629\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ property\ and\ return\ the\ largest\ configured\ column\ width}}

\DoxyCodeLine{07644\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ configured\ cell\ padding}}
